- `P.1`
  Equation:

  Variable legend: `X^(phys)` tracks containment geometry, phase, pressure, and seal integrity.

  Confidence: mixed

  Variable legend: `u` is the wave profile; `U_line` is the contraction-compatible update.
  Reading: root fixation / essence load / fluid carriage line.

### Hacking Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{P_1}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{P_1}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})\le B_{\mathrm{P_1}}\]

  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.
  Reading: root fixation / essence load / fluid carriage line.
  Confidence: mixed

- `P.10`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{P_10}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{P_10}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{P_10}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{P_10}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{P_10}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{P_10}})\le B_{\mathrm{P_10}}\]

  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.
  Reading: essence load / extraction circuit / circulation circuit line.
  Confidence: mixed

- `P.11`

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: root fixation / essence load / fluid carriage line.
  Confidence: mixed

  Equation:

## Direct Operational Meaning

This page is a STAR-MARKED RECIPE - a pharmaceutical formula where marginal stars serve as PROGRESS MARKERS. Each star corresponds to a stage of the recipe, and the star's visual properties (solid, hollow, red-dotted) encode what TYPE of operation occurs at that stage. Think of the stars as a...

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f106r` behaves as a `star formulary` with 19 retort/transmutation events and 94 completion markers distributed across 47 visible lines.

## Mythic Extraction

Across the mythic lenses, `f106r` is one training station in the Book V fire curriculum: star recipe - progressive crystallization.
